# UI Registry — Glossary

> Source: `tokens/ui-registry.json` (version `0.1.0`).
> Generated by `npm run ui-registry:build`. Do not edit by hand.
>
> This glossary is the human-readable companion to the test-id constants in `tokens/build/test-ids.ts`. Both come from the same source.

## Why this exists

Per the Executable-Requirements PRD (`tokens/templates/PRD-Executable-Requirements-Gherkin-Component-Paths.docx.md`), every UI element referenced from a Jira ticket — and from every Gherkin scenario — uses a **stable path** instead of a description. `component.checkout.cart.checkoutButton` is the contract; the visual, the position, and the generated test-id are not.

## Screens

| Path | Description | test-id |
|---|---|---|
| `screen.landing.home` | Landing page at / (Gherkin: screen.landing) | `screen-landing-home` |
| `screen.contact.page` | Contact / demo booking at /contact (Gherkin: screen.contact) | `screen-contact-page` |
| `screen.howItWorks.page` | How it works at /how-it-works (Gherkin: screen.howItWorks) | `screen-howItWorks-page` |
